# Research Log

Daily pre-market research entries are appended below by the `pre-market` routine.

## Entry Schema

```
## YYYY-MM-DD — Pre-market Research

### Account
- Equity: $X
- Cash: $X
- Buying power: $X
- Daytrade count: N

### Market Context
- WTI / Brent oil:
- S&P 500 futures:
- VIX:
- Today's catalysts:
- Earnings before open:
- Economic calendar:
- Sector momentum:

### Trade Ideas
Listed in R:R-descending order (tie-break: ticker ascending). One numbered line per idea, format:
1. **ID:** `pm-YYYY-MM-DD-TICKER` — TICKER, catalyst, entry $X, stop $X, target $X, R:R X:1, planned trail percent: 10
2. ...

### Risk Factors
- ...

### Decision
TRADE or HOLD (default HOLD if no edge)

### Sources
- Perplexity citations: <list>
- WebSearch fallback used: yes/no (which queries)
```

---

## 2026-04-27 — Pre-market Research (refreshed)

*Prior 2026-04-27 entry refreshed: corrected SPX futures level, added FOMC Wed Apr 29 + Big Tech earnings (MSFT/GOOG) Wed which were missing from prior version. Original preserved in git history (commit abf37e7).*

### Account
- Equity: $10,000.00
- Cash: $10,000.00
- Buying power: $20,000.00
- Daytrade count: 0
- Positions: none | Open orders: none
- Note: Alpaca account shows `options_trading_level: 3` — irrelevant per hard rule "NO OPTIONS, ever"; wrapper kill-switch + buy-side gate (stocks only) prevent any options path.

### Market Context
- WTI: ~$92–94/bbl (Apr 23 close ~$92.92; prediction markets imply ~$94 today). Brent: not directly quoted today; recent ~$105 area, softer on supply talk.
- S&P 500 futures: E-mini ~6,865 area in premarket (+2 pts); SPX cash 6,824.66 last close after 7-day up streak. Premarket flat-to-slightly-up. NDX futures +48, Dow futures -2.
- VIX: 19.31 (Apr 23 close), range 18.87–19.50 — calm regime.
- Today's catalysts: Dallas Fed Manufacturing Survey 10:30 AM ET. VZ earnings BMO. Otherwise light.
- Earnings before open: VZ (Verizon) is the marquee BMO name; smaller: SSYS (Stratasys), BH (Biglari), GWRS, UFI, EARN. After close: minor.
- This-week event risk (high): **FOMC statement + Powell presser Wed Apr 29 (2:00 / 2:30 PM ET)**; **MSFT + GOOG earnings Wed Apr 29 (most likely AMC)**; META/AMZN/AAPL likely later in week; ECI Q1 Thu Apr 30.
- 10Y yield: 4.289% (~unch). Crude/Brent/natgas softer overnight.
- Sector momentum YTD (recent reads): Energy leading (~+26% YTD, oil-firm + AI-power demand); Industrials #2 (~+9–16%, defense/AI infra); Consumer Staples #3 (~+10%); Tech/Semis still strong with IT +45% forward EPS revisions.

### Trade Ideas
*(v1 paper — kill-switch active, documentation only; verify live prices at v2 market-open before any entry. With FOMC + Big Tech earnings Wed, prudent stance is to defer fresh entries until post-event.)*

1. **XLE** — Energy sector remains YTD leader; oil firm in low-$90s; non-binary, sector-ETF avoids single-name event risk. Indicative entry ~$95, stop ~$85.50 (-10%), target ~$114 (+20%), R:R ~2:1.
2. **XLI** — Industrials #2 YTD; defense + AI-infrastructure tailwind, not directly exposed to MSFT/GOOG print. Indicative entry ~$160, stop ~$144 (-10%), target ~$192 (+20%), R:R ~2:1.
3. **SMH** — Semis broad ETF; AI capex thesis intact, but **carries indirect Big-Tech-earnings spillover Wed**. Indicative entry ~$295, stop ~$265.50 (-10%), target ~$354 (+20%), R:R ~2:1. Prefer waiting until after MSFT/GOOG print.

Buy-side gate (forward check): all three pass position count (0/6), trades-this-week (0/3), 20%-cap, sector-momentum, stock-only. Final cash / PDT check belongs at execution.

### Risk Factors
- **Macro / event:** FOMC Wed is the dominant risk; any hawkish surprise hits multiples broadly. Powell tone matters more than statement.
- **Earnings concentration:** ~40% of S&P 500 market cap reports this week; MSFT/GOOG Wed dictate sentiment for tech and semis.
- **Sector:** Energy headline risk if US–Iran/OPEC+ talk deflates oil; semis stretched after multi-quarter run.
- **Idiosyncratic:** Single-name high-priced AI plays (AVGO, etc.) breach 20% cap on $10K account; favor sector ETFs.
- **Liquidity:** Pre-FOMC, Mon–Tue chop is common; thin conviction trades tend to underperform.

### Decision
**HOLD** — Day 1, v1 paper-only, kill-switch active. Even ignoring the kill-switch, the rational stance is to wait through FOMC (Wed) and Big Tech prints before deploying capital. Patience > activity.

### Trade Ideas
Listed in R:R-descending order (tie-break: ticker ascending). One numbered line per idea, format:

1. **ID:** `pm-2026-06-12-GE` — **tier:** satellite, GE (General Electric / GE Aerospace, Industrials sector), catalyst: **50s-RS matured through binary cycle** — Tue's razor-thin +0.60pp expanded to +3.82pp by Fri PM (3.22pp gain through hot-CPI Wed + friendly-PPI Thu — durable regime confirmation); 10s-RS held +5.95pp; XLI sector +12% YTD leading-quadrant per Vantage / +13.1% trailing 6mo per Schwab; XLI A&D 24% weight (GE is top-3 XLI constituent — aerospace cycle + AI-power-infrastructure tailwind); Industrials sector demonstrated Wed-Thu rotation resilience (XLI +3.46% Thu, GE held flat through binaries while NVDA/AVGO worsened); entry $332.76, stop $282.85 (stop width 15% → risk-parity sizing: equity $10,006.98, 2% risk = $200.14; `sizing.py size --equity 10006.98 --price 332.76 --stop-frac 0.15` = **4 sh = $1,331.04 = 13.30% of equity** (well below 20% cap; Industrials slot 2/2 satellites)), target $440.00, R:R 2.15:1, planned trail percent: 15

### Risk Factors
- **Macro / FOMC Jun 16–17 next Wed:** Week's next binary — Fed expected to deliver one more 25bp cut in 2026 (per yesterday's research). Hot CPI + friendly PPI mix leaves rate path ambiguous; hawkish FOMC could re-test cyclicals (Industrials including GE). Position is held through weekend + Mon + Tue before binary lands — entry today gives 2.5 sessions of price discovery before binary. GE 15% stop width vs CAT's 10% reflects the wider vol regime + binary proximity.
- **Industrials concentration cap (binding soft constraint):** After GE fill: XLI $1,933.25 + CAT $1,813.42 + GE $1,331.04 = $5,077.71 = **55.97% of new-deployed ($9,071.83)**. Industrials satellite slots: **2/2 ✓ at cap** (CAT + GE). ETF core floor: $5,927.37 / $9,071.83 = **65.34%** ≥ 45% ✓ (held intact). Buy-side gate passes structurally; sector-concentration risk is material — a Rule 10 sector-kill on Industrials (2 consecutive failed trades) would close 3 positions at once.
- **Michigan Sentiment 10:00 ET today (35min after market open):** Consensus ~44.8 (UMich page shows actual already at 44.8 prelim — print may have leaked or been pre-released). Weak read = consumer recession risk → cyclical sell-off → GE/XLI/CAT downside. Strong read = relief bid → cyclical lift. Asymmetric event 30 min into trading.
- **OPEC Monthly Report today:** XLE-specific catalyst. WTI Jul 26 −1.14% premarket — soft tape continuing. If OPEC report signals oversupply / dovish demand, XLE cushion (2.20% — book's tightest) could trip on Fri close. Independent of GE entry.
- **VIX 19.44 (compressed from 22.22 CPI peak):** Vol regime stepping down post-CPI/PPI digest. Spreads tightening, intraday whip risk normalizing. GE 15% stop width reflects yesterday's elevated regime — adequate margin in today's normalizing tape.
- **GE 10s-RS compression risk:** +5.95pp Fri vs +6.88pp Tue — mild compression (−0.93pp) but durable. 50s-RS strengthened materially through binary cycle. Asymmetric: GE held through CPI/PPI better than AVGO/NVDA which both worsened on the same window.
- **Friday + weekend gap risk:** Entry today means weekend macro/geopolitical risk (Mid-East tensions, oil-tape headlines, EU/Asia weekend news). Mitigation: 15% stop width + risk-parity sizing bounds Mon-open gap risk to ~2% of equity worst case.
- **Held book idiosyncratic:** CAT recovered from Wed's 1.14% cushion → 6.65%; Rule 16 decay chain broken (Thu flag=0). XLE cushion 2.20% — book's tightest, oil-tape downside risk acute. XLI/XLB cushions 9.57%/8.94% — clear.
- **Liquidity / event-risk:** GE $1.5B ADV solid; spreads expected to be normal at open absent surprise Michigan print. Open-quote stale-risk minimal post-PPI; Wed's CPI-related stale-quote conditions have normalized.

### Decision
**TRADE** — 1 satellite idea (GE) confirmed; XLK deferred.

Rationale: (1) **GE 50s-RS matured** — Tue's razor-thin +0.60pp expanded to +3.82pp Fri PM through hot-CPI Wed + friendly-PPI Thu binary cycle = durable regime confirmation (the v3 deferral path validated yesterday's HOLD and today's TRADE); (2) **GE held through binaries while NVDA/AVGO worsened** — clear relative-strength demonstration on the same window (GE 10s +3.72% vs NVDA −4.27% vs AVGO −9.61%); (3) **Industrials sector leading-quadrant unchanged** — XLI +3.46% Thu, sector rotation intact; (4) **All buy-side gates pass with margin** — position $1,331 = 13.30% equity, core floor 65.34% post-fill, Industrials 2/2 satellites at cap, 0/5 weekly trades remaining; (5) **VIX compressed to 19.44** from 22.22 CPI-peak — vol regime stepping back down, spreads/whip risk normalizing; (6) **Patience > activity tradeoff:** v3 was designed to capture exactly this single-stock setup — confirmed RS through binary cycle is the high-conviction signal we deferred Wed pre-print to await; deferring further into FOMC adds binary-stacking without further information gain on GE-specific thesis.

Counter-rationale (acknowledged risks): (a) Industrials concentration 56% of deployed post-fill is material — Rule 10 sector-kill on Industrials would trigger a 3-position liquidation; (b) FOMC Jun 17 binary 3 sessions out — Mon/Tue tape + binary day before lockout; (c) Friday/weekend gap risk; (d) XLE cushion 2.20% on independent oil-tape risk. Net: gates pass, setup matured, vol regime cooperating — proceed with sized 4 sh @ 15% stop width per `sizing.py size` to bound downside.

Market-open will attempt GE limit-with-slippage entry; stop NOT placed at entry (Rule 13 — daily-summary T 15:00 CT places trailing-stop 15%). Midday will evaluate Rule 16 decay on held book + any GE intraday Rule 7. Telegram silent unless macro-urgent (OPEC oil shock or Michigan extreme print would trigger; baseline silent).

Carry-forward deferred candidates into Mon Jun 15 pre-market re-screen:
- `pm-2026-06-12-XLK` — defer 1 more session (core, Tech ETF) — 10s-RS razor-thin +0.28pp re-flipped positive; needs +1pp expansion to confirm. Pre-FOMC binary risk argues for waiting.
- `pm-2026-06-12-NVDA` — defer (satellite, Tech) — 10s-RS worsened −1.19pp → −2.03pp + marginal 50-DMA breach.
- `pm-2026-06-12-AVGO` — defer further (satellite, Tech) — DOUBLE FAIL deteriorating; needs both DMA repair (~$20 below 50-DMA) + 10s-RS rebound (~7pp from −7.38pp).
- `pm-2026-06-12-MPC` — defer (satellite, Energy) — 50s-RS fails; Energy slot already used by XLE.
- `pm-2026-06-12-XLU` — **RETIRE** from carryforward (core, Utilities ETF) — DEAD path triple fail; rate regime reversal required to re-arm.
